q0#####SELECT     COUNT(*) FROM     postHistory as ph,     posts as p,     users as u,     badges as b WHERE     b.UserId = u.Id     AND p.OwnerUserId = u.Id     AND ph.UserId = u.Id     AND ph.CreationDate >= '2013-04-27 18:08:19' :: timestamp     AND ph.CreationDate <= '2016-06-15 08:22:43' :: timestamp     AND p.PostTypeId = 2;

q987#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		postHistory as ph,  		badges as b,          votes as v,          users as u  where u.Id =b.UserId 	and b.UserId = ph.UserId 	and ph.UserId = v.UserId 	and v.UserId = c.UserId  AND b.Date<='2014-09-11 20:15:50'::timestamp  AND c.Score=1  AND ph.PostHistoryTypeId=5  AND ph.CreationDate<='2014-08-17 22:57:13'::timestamp  AND u.Views>=0  AND u.Views<=260  AND u.UpVotes=0  AND v.VoteTypeId=2;
q988#####select  count(*) from postHistory as ph,          votes as v,  		users as u,  		badges as b  where u.Id = ph.UserId 	and u.Id = v.UserId 	and u.Id = b.UserId  AND b.Date>='2010-07-26 20:58:42'::timestamp  AND ph.CreationDate>='2011-02-10 17:53:56'::timestamp  AND u.Reputation=8  AND u.CreationDate>='2011-03-20 18:45:06'::timestamp  AND v.CreationDate>='2010-07-23 00:00:00'::timestamp;
q989#####select  count(*) from posts as p,  		postLinks as pl,          postHistory as ph where p.Id = pl.PostId 	and pl.PostId = ph.PostId  AND pl.LinkTypeId=1  AND p.CommentCount>=0  AND p.CreationDate<='2014-08-21 21:10:55'::timestamp;
q990#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		posts as p,           postHistory as ph,  		badges as b,          users as u  where u.Id = c.UserId 	and u.Id = p.LastEditorUserId 	and u.Id = ph.UserId 	and u.Id = b.UserId  AND c.Score=0  AND ph.PostHistoryTypeId=2  AND p.PostTypeId=2  AND p.ViewCount>=0  AND p.ViewCount<=2291  AND p.FavoriteCount>=0  AND p.FavoriteCount<=7  AND u.UpVotes<=17;
q991#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		posts as p,  		votes as v,         users as u  where p.Id = c.PostId 	and p.Id = v.PostId 	and u.id = p.LastEditorUserId  AND c.Score=0  AND c.CreationDate>='2010-07-20 05:53:59'::timestamp  AND u.Reputation>=1  AND u.Views>=0  AND u.Views<=64  AND v.CreationDate<='2014-09-10 00:00:00'::timestamp;
q992#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		posts as p,  		postLinks as pl,          postHistory as ph,          votes as v  where p.Id = c.PostId 	and p.Id = pl.PostId     and p.Id = ph.PostId     and p.Id = v.PostId  AND c.CreationDate>='2010-08-18 18:42:14'::timestamp  AND c.CreationDate<='2014-09-02 21:45:21'::timestamp  AND ph.CreationDate<='2014-08-03 15:42:03'::timestamp  AND pl.CreationDate>='2011-03-22 09:17:06'::timestamp  AND p.Score<=17  AND p.FavoriteCount>=0  AND p.CreationDate<='2014-09-10 20:04:07'::timestamp  AND v.VoteTypeId=2;
q993#####select  count(*) from badges as b, 		posts as p where b.UserId = p.OwnerUserId  AND b.Date>='2010-07-27 11:43:44'::timestamp  AND p.AnswerCount>=0  AND p.CreationDate>='2010-08-16 11:36:42'::timestamp  AND p.CreationDate<='2014-09-13 23:46:05'::timestamp;
q994#####select  count(*) from postLinks as pl,          posts as p,  		users as u,  		badges as b  where p.Id = pl.RelatedPostId  	and u.Id = p.OwnerUserId 	and u.Id = b.UserId  AND b.Date>='2010-08-01 11:24:55'::timestamp  AND pl.LinkTypeId=1  AND pl.CreationDate<='2014-07-25 09:28:48'::timestamp  AND u.DownVotes<=0  AND u.UpVotes=0;
q995#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		posts as p,          users as u where c.UserId = u.Id 	and u.Id = p.OwnerUserId  AND p.ViewCount>=0  AND p.CommentCount>=0  AND p.CommentCount<=7  AND p.FavoriteCount>=0  AND p.CreationDate>='2010-08-09 03:57:50'::timestamp  AND u.UpVotes>=0  AND u.UpVotes<=20;
q996#####select  count(*) from badges as b, 		posts as p where b.UserId = p.OwnerUserId  AND p.PostTypeId=2;
q997#####select  count(*) from comments as c,  		posts as p,          postHistory as ph,          votes as v,          badges as b,          users as u  where u.Id = p.OwnerUserId     and u.Id = b.UserId     and p.Id = c.PostId     and p.Id = ph.PostId     and p.Id = v.PostId  AND b.Date>='2010-07-29 20:04:10'::timestamp  AND c.CreationDate>='2009-04-12 07:48:50'::timestamp  AND c.CreationDate<='2014-09-12 14:48:38'::timestamp  AND ph.PostHistoryTypeId=2  AND ph.CreationDate<='2014-08-30 17:38:38'::timestamp  AND p.CommentCount>=0  AND p.CommentCount<=15  AND p.FavoriteCount<=10  AND u.CreationDate>='2011-08-18 14:53:56'::timestamp;
q998#####SELECT     COUNT(*) FROM     postHistory as ph,     posts as p,     users as u,     badges as b WHERE     b.UserId = u.Id     AND p.OwnerUserId = u.Id     AND ph.UserId = u.Id     AND ph.CreationDate >= '2009-09-27 18:08:19' :: timestamp     AND ph.CreationDate <= '2012-12-10 08:22:43' :: timestamp     AND p.PostTypeId = 2;
q999#####select  count(*) from comments as c,          postHistory as ph,  		badges as b,          users as u  where u.Id = c.UserId 	and u.Id = ph.UserId 	and u.Id = b.UserId  AND ph.PostHistoryTypeId=25;
